Research shows that many of the graduated students, don’t know the opportunities they can avail through shrouded skills, which were never known. They lack professional and technical skills because their courses cannot cover most of the things. Student needs to be socially aware, they should have knowledge how to implement things in practical life.
AqdaarNation is a student based society, which connects professionally and technically skilled students of different universities to build the understanding of professional, technical and social awareness among their circles. It informs about the job and internship opportunities to different university students. It helps to build networking, awareness, professional skills, technical skills and much more.

28/02/2020, 12:28 - +92 307 2254474: By #professor #intekhab #alam sahb
One  of the renownd medical specialist.. 

Some facts about Corona virus.....
If you have a runny nose and sputum when you have a cold, you are probably not suffering from coronavirus infection; because coronavirus pneumonia leads to dry cough without runny nose. This is the simplest clinical way to differentiate  between simple flu and Corona infection.
The Wuhan Corona virus is not heat-resistant and will be killed at a temperature of 26-27 degrees. Therefore, hot drinks and sunlight exposure is likely to kill the virus. Drinking warm water is effective for all viruses anyway. However, remember, avoid taking chilled or iced water.
Following are some other advices and informations about Coronavirus:
1. It is pretty large in size (cell is about 400-500nm diameter), so any normal mask (not just the  N95 feature) should be able to filter it out. However, when someone who's infected sneezes in front of you, it will take a great 3 meters (about 10 feet) before it drops to the ground and is no longer airborne. 

2. When the virus drops on metal surface, it will live for at least 12 hours. So remember if you come in contact with any metal surface, wash your hands with soap thoroughly. 

3. The virus can remain active on fabric for 6-12 hours. Normal laundry detergent should kill the virus. For winter clothing that does not require daily washing, you can put it out under the sun to kill the virus. 

About the symptoms of the pneumonia caused by Coronavirus:

1. It will first infect the throat, so the throat will have the dry sore throat feeling which will last for 3 to 4 days

2. Then the virus will blend into the nasal fluid and drips into the trachea and enter the lungs, causing pneumonia. This process will take 5 to 6 days.    

3. With pneumonia, comes high fever and difficulty in breathing. The nasal congestion is not like the normal kind. You will feel like you are drowning in water. It's important to go seek immediate medical attention if you feel like this. 

About prevention:

1. The most common way of getting infected is by touching things in public, so you must wash your hands frequently. The virus can only live on your hands for 5-10 mins, but a lot can happen in those 5-10 mins (you can rub your eyes or pick your nose unwittingly).

2. Aside from washing your hands frequently, you can gargle with Betadine Sore Throat Gargle to eliminate or minimize the germs while they are still in your throat (before dripping down to your lungs). 

Folks, take extra care and drink plenty of warm water.

(Source; Prof. Dr Intikhab Alam renowned medical specialist)

“

ر سے رویورس سیکسزم (مردوں کےخلاف جنسی تعصب)

"صرف فیملیز کے لئے؟ یہ ریورس سیکس ازم ہے! "
"تندور کی لائن میں عورت پہلے جاتی ہے"
"مردوں کو دہی اور راشن لینے جانا پڑتا ہے یار کوئی یہ نہیں دیکھتا"

خواتین کے لئے روٹی کی لائن کاٹنا کیوں ٹھیک ہے جب کہ پہلے آنے والے مرد زیادہ انتظار کرتے ہیں؟ بس میں سیٹیں خواتین کے لئے الگ کیوں ہیں؟ بازار سے ہرا دھنیا لانے کے لئے ماؤں کو اپنے بیٹوں کے پیچھے کیوں بھاگنا پڑتا ہے؟

لیکن اگر ہم ذرا غور کریں تو پتہ چلتا ہے کہ یہ نظام کسی نہ کسی طرح سے مردوں کو فائدہ پہنچا رہا ہوتا ہے۔

تندور کے لیے قطار میں کھڑے ہونے پر خواتین کو ہراساں کیا جاتا ہے، انہیں روٹی پہلے دے دینا اس مسئلے کو حل کرنے کی کوشش ہے۔ یہی بات بسوں میں ترجیحی نشستوں پر بھی لاگو ہوتی ہے - کتنی خواتین اپنے جسموں پر ہاتھ دھرنے کی وجہ سے پبلک ٹرانسپورٹ کا استعمال بھی نہیں کرسکتی ہیں؟ اور اہل خانہ اپنے بیٹوں کو، اپنی بیٹیوں کو "محفوظ" رکھنے کے لئے، راشن خریدنے بھیجتے رہتے ہیں (حالانکہ گھریلو تشدد پر نظر ڈالنے سے ان کا نقطہ نظر کچھ تبدیل ہوسکتا ہے)، لیکن اس نام نہاد حفاظت اور بازار میں کچھ دوروں کے بدلے میں، خواتین گھر کے سارے کام مستقل طور پر ہر وقت کرتے ہوئے اس “احسان” کی قیمت چکانی پڑتی ہے۔ 

خواتین اور غیر بائنری افراد بھی مردوں کے لئے متعصب  ہو سکتے ہیں لیکن ان کا تعصب نظامی یا  حسب رواج نہیں ہے۔ ان کا تعصب خلا میں ہوتا ہے اور اکثر مظلومیت کا ایک ردعمل ہوتا ہے۔ دوسری طرف ، جب مرد خواتین کے خلاف تعصب رکھتے ہیں تو ، وہ اپنے آپ کو فائدہ پہنچانے کے لئے نظام کو تبدیل کرتے ہیں۔ وہ اپنے تعصبات کو استعمال کرنے کے لئے معاشی ، سیاسی ، اور معاشرتی ڈھانچے پر اپنے قابو کا استعمال کرتے ہیں۔

یہ آسان ہے؛ جنسی تعصب ایک ساختی عمل ہے جہاں معاشرے کے اداروں کو کسی پر ظلم کرنے کے لئے استعمال کیا جاتا ہے۔ چونکہ خواتین ، خواجہ سرا، اور غیر ثنائی افراد ان اداروں پر قابو نہیں رکھتے ہیں ، لہذا مردوں کے خلاف ریورس  جنسی تعصب موجود ہی نہیں ہے۔

https://www.piaic.org/

We have waived the entry test requirement and the fees for the next three months (First Quarter) for the following four courses:
1. Artificial Intelligence (AI)
2. Cloud Native and Mobile Web Computing
3. Internet of Things (IoT)
4. Blockchain

These courses are designed for absolute beginners and you will be able to learn online at your conviniance while sitting at home.

استاد : اگر تمہارے پاس 86،400 روپے ہوں اور کوئی ڈاکو ان میں سے 10 روپےچھین کر بھاگ جائے تو تم کیا کرو گے ؟*

کیا تم اُس کے پیچھے بھاگ کر اپنی لوٹی ہوئی 10 روپےکی رقم واپس حاصل کرنے کی کوشش کرو گے ؟؟ یا پھر اپنے باقی کے بچے ہوئے 86،390 روپےکو حفاظت سے لیکر اپنے راستے پر چلتے رہو گے؟

طلبا نے کہا : ہم 10 روپے کی حقیر رقم کو نظر انداز کرتے ہوئے اپنے باقی کے پیسوں کو حفاظت سے لیکر اپنے راستے پر چلتے رہیں گے۔

استاد نے کہا : تمھارا بیان اور مشاہدہ درست نہیں۔ میں نے دیکھا ہے کہ ذیادہ تر لوگ اُن 10 روپے کو واپس لینے کے چکر میں ڈاکو کا پیچھا کرتے ہیں اور نتیجے کے طور پر اپنے باقی کے بچے ہوئے 86،390 روپے سے بھی ہاتھ دھو بیٹھتے ہیں۔

طلباء نے حیرت سے استاد کو دیکھتے ہوئے کہا: سر، یہ ناممکن ہے، ایسا کون کرتا ہے ؟

استاد نے کہا : یہ 86،400 اصل میں ہمارے ایک دن کے سیکنڈز ہیں۔

کسی 10 سیکنڈز کی بات کو لیکر، یا کسی 10 سیکنڈز کی ناراضگی اور غصے کو بنیاد بنا کر ہم باقی کا سارا دن سوچنے، جلنے اور کُڑھنے میں گزار کر اپنا باقی کا سارا دن برباد کرتے ہیں۔ یہ والے 10 سیکنڈز ہمارے باقی بچے ہوئے 86،390 سیکنڈز کو بھی کھا کر برباد کر دیتے ہیں۔

باتوں کو نظرانداز کرنا سیکھیئے۔ ایسا نہ ہو کہ آپ کا کوئی وقتی اشتعال، ناراضگی آپ سے آپ کے سارے دن کی طاقت چھین کر لے جائے.

معاف کریں, بھول جائیں اور آگے بڑھیں....!!

10/09/2020, 18:27 - +92 333 3926926: To,
Student Advisor 

        University of Karachi.

Respected Sir, 
We , the student of UOK, are writing this request letter, to bring to your kind attention towards a  very serious reservations which the students of UBIT dept. have on the notification relating to final exams, since the students of UOK believe that this new development may significantly impact final academic results of the students for the upcoming semester. 

1.	As you are aware that students have been taught online throughout the semester and they prepared and learned everything while keeping in mind that the exams will be conducted online and in open book format. So, if there will be any sudden change in the policy, this will definitely affect the grades of students. 

2.	Most of the students (around 40%) live in hostels of the university. And around 3 to 4 students are accommodated in one room, and according to government’s policy “no more than one student is allowed in a room in hostel”, due to this issue such students will have to face accommodation issues. 

3.	Majority of the students use shuttle services for the purpose of transportation, as the charges for uber/Careem services cannot be paid by all of the individuals, students may face transportation issues also.

4.	 Some of the students are out of country, due to COVID situation it will be difficult for them to arrive Karachi. 

5.    UET Lahore recently asked students for physical classes and it was reported that 3 students are suspected to be patients of coronavirus, if such kind of unfortunate event occurs to the students of Karachi university, it will put other student’s LIFE also at RISK. 

To sum up, it is submitted that all of the above issues have disturbed the study schedule of the students very badly and due to passage of considerable time (i.e. 12 weeks out of 14 weeks) and given the time constraints it will be impractical to prepare for physical exams. It is also submitted that students are of the view that conducting exams physically would be very unfair as it will have significant impact on final results of students as well as mental and physical health of students. 

In view of the above, it is therefore humbly requested to please consider conducting the final exams of In open book form/online. 

Regards, 
Students of UOK.

Send this at studentadvisor@uok.edu.pk

Only change the depart name

16/09/2020, 01:00 - +92 347 8302568: 1.	As you are aware that students have been taught online throughout the semester and they prepared and learned everything while keeping in mind that the exams will be conducted online and in open book format. So, if there will be any sudden change in the policy, this will definitely affect the grades of students. 

2.	Most of the students (around 40%) live in hostels of the university. And around 3 to 4 students are accommodated in one room, and according to government’s policy “no more than one student is allowed in a room in hostel”, due to this issue such students will have to face accommodation issues. 

3.	Majority of the students use shuttle services for the purpose of transportation, as the charges for uber/Careem services cannot be paid by all of the individuals, students may face transportation issues also.

4.	 Some of the students are out of country, due to COVID situation it will be difficult for them to arrive Karachi. 

5.    UET Lahore recently asked students for physical classes and it was reported that 3 students are suspected to be patients of coronavirus, if such kind of unfortunate event occurs to the students of Karachi university, it will put other student’s LIFE also at RISK. 

To sum up, it is submitted that all of the above issues have disturbed the study schedule of the students very badly and due to passage of considerable time (i.e. 12 weeks out of 14 weeks) and given the time constraints it will be impractical to prepare for physical exams. It is also submitted that students are of the view that conducting exams physically would be very unfair as it will have significant impact on final results of students as well as mental and physical health of students. 

In view of the above, it is therefore humbly requested to please consider conducting the final exams of In open book form/assignment based/online.

25/03/2021, 19:45 - +92 347 8302568: *Looking to master the Node.JS ?* 

Node.JS is an open-source, cross-platform Javascript runtime environment. It has allowed millions of frontend developers to code server-sider as well without the need to learn a completely different language. Where Node really shines is in building fast, scalable, real-time applications, as it’s capable of handling a huge number of simultaneous connections with high throughput, which equates to high scalability. Due to its event-driven, asynchronous, non-blocking and single-threaded nature, it is highly memory efficient and rapidly fast.

*Webicamp* offers a 4-month-long online module that is highly comprehensive, exploring all the essential areas of Node.JS in depth. It adopts a project based approach which includes building a real world MERN stack based Apps.

22/08/2021, 13:24 - Houra: Hi Career Service Office,

My Name is Huzaifa Bin Sadiq, and I am working as Principal technical Consultant at Infotech Australia and New Zealand. I would like to give you a brief introduction of the company before moving forward.

WHO WE ARE We’re? 
A software development & consulting firm specializing in industry-specific solutions. 

WHAT WE DO 
We help senior executives in Utilities and Local Government get more from their IT systems, by centralising data, streamlining processing, and reducing complexity. We do this through business-specific solutions based on industry-specific consulting and industry-best technologies. 

HOW iTANZ WORKS 
Instead of developing comprehensive bespoke solutions each time or combining point solutions that leave gaps, we’ve taken industry-best frameworks like Oracle and purpose-built solutions for specific industries. This way, executives in Utilities and Councils gain the precise visibility and functionality they need, without costly professional services or endless variations. 

HOW WE’RE DIFFERENT 
iTANZ solutions are designed for both IT and business users. Our solutions integrate with existing data sources to provide unequalled visibility and clarity for senior executives, who can run the solutions easily themselves. As new systems involve change, our solutions include training and best practice processes to encourage rapid uptake by staff. 

WHY IT MATTERS 
In industries like Utilities, Local Government & Manufacturing, information is fragmented into various systems. As a result, senior executives have to piece together fragments to gain a rough idea of reality. With an iTANZ solution, they gain a single, accurate, real-time view of their combined data sources, so they can make better decisions sooner, improve their service to customers and devise more accurate plans. 

WHAT OTHERS SAY 
“Getting software in is one thing; managing the people and processes to make it work is something else. iTANZ’s training and hand-holding made the transition smooth and fast.” - Peter Larsson, Project Manager, Automotive Parts Manufacturer. 
LIKE TO KNOW MORE? If you’d like improve visibility, customer service and operations, find out more www.itanz.com.au

During last couple of years, we started our services in Pakistani Market and currently we have representation in three countries Pakistan, Australia and Saudi Arabia. In every year we have graduate trainee program in fall which is at the same time when most of the fresh graduates passed out from the universities. Currently we are planning to have 2-4 graduate trainees in our team, this number might go up in future. To be specific we are looking for 2 graduate trainees for Data Analytics & Data Engineering and 2 graduate trainees for software development & Integrations.


Other than graduate trainee program we also hire senior and junior resources for different domains e.g., Software Development, System Integration, Mobile Application Development, Analytics & DWH and for application functional consultancy roles. 

I would like to request you to join hands with us to provide us quality resources, initially targeting the fresh graduate of this year or last year so we can work it out on their career path. In this regard if Career Service Office provide us graduate profiles with their brief introduction it will be a good help for us to find out the right talent. 

Our Graduate Trainee Program,

At iTANZ we hire fresh graduates as Graduate trainee Officer and provide them a chance to learn the technology they love; we offer them an opportunity to get certified in the core technologies within 6 months. After 6 months we offer them permanent position in our organization with perks and benefits.

During the trainee program, we offer 45K to 55K to the trainees depending on their academics and evaluation. 

Please send the CV’s at Huzaifa.sadiq@itanzgroup.com

I wish you the best of luck!

Department of Computer Science - UBIT continued the legacy of hosting the "Annual Dinner", an official meet & greet for the students, teachers and the alumni of UBIT, organized under the supervision of Chairman and faculty of UBIT. This substantial event was defined by the department’s former students and has been carried out for years.

AD is itself an exclusive platform for everyone to grow their networks, interact with the dearest teachers and make countless memories with friends as well.

This spectacular evening starts with the red carpet and as the night goes on there are arrays of skits and performances by the students from First Year to Final Year, job fair, lavish dinner, title distribution to teachers and students, special performances and much more untold.
